73	3rd Street and Superior Avenue and as identified on the attached map (Map Change No. 2534).
81	Be it ordained by the Council of the City of Cleveland:
81	Section 1. That the Use District of lands bounded and described as follows:
81	Beginning at the intersection of West 6th Street and St. Clair Avenue;
81	Thence easterly along the centerline of St. Clair Avenue to its intersection with the centerline of West 3rd Street;
81	Thence southerly along said centerline to its intersection with the centerline of Superior Avenue;
81	Thence westerly along said centerline to its intersection with the centerline of West 6th Street;
81	Thence northerly along said centerline to the place of origin;
73	And as identified on the attached map shall be established as an Urban Core Overlay District;
81	Section 2. That the change of zoning of lands described in Section 1 shall be identified as Map Change No. 2534, and
73	shall be made upon the Building Zone Maps of the City of Cleveland on file in the office of the Clerk of Council and on
73	file in the office of the City Planning Commission by the appropriate person designated for this purpose by the City Plan-
73	ning Commission.
81	Section 3. That this ordinance shall take effect and be in force from and after the earliest period allowed by law.
